圣歌=Holy Song
{{A}}的特殊战斗资源，用于提升『贯穿时空的轮转』的技能效果与减少释放『华光下的治愈诗』后所需的准备时间。={{A}}'s special resource, used to increase the skill effect of [Wheel of Time] and decrease [Poem of Radiance] preparation time.
<color\=#66ccff>总伤害增幅</color>=<color\=#66ccff>Total DMG Amp</color>
所有伤害的最终增幅效果，此效果为独立加成。=Increase Final DMG Amp of all damage. This effect is an independent bonus.

<color\=#66ccff>特定召唤顺序</color>=<color\=#66ccff>Specific Summon Order</color>
未同时拥有四种蔬菜骑士时，按照茄子骑士、马铃薯骑士、蘑菇骑士、芦笋骑士的顺序进行召唤；已同时拥有四种蔬菜骑士时，后续仅召唤马铃薯骑士。\n透过『蔬菜骑士·集合』首次召唤茄子骑士时，{{A}}自动变幻为『茄之紫』状态。=When YUI doesn't have 4 kinds of Vegetable Knights, summon them in the order of Eggplant Knight, Potato Knight, Mushroom Knight, Asparagus Knight; When YUI has 4 kinds of Vegetable Knights, she will only summon Potato Knights.\nWhen YUI summon Eggplant Knight from [Vegetable Knights: Assemble] for the first time, change to [Eggplant Purple].
<color\=#66ccff>特定规则</color>=<color\=#66ccff>Specific Rules</color>
按下述优先顺序，{{A}}在释放HIGHLIGHT后会触发处于不同状态下的『蔬菜骑士·出击』：\n1、HIGHLIGHT目标未处于『蘑菇孢子』状态下，且自身拥有蘑菇骑士时，触发处于『菇之粉』状态的『蔬菜骑士·出击』；\n2、自身未处于『块茎之力』状态下，且自身拥有马铃薯骑士时，触发处于『薯之黄』状态的『蔬菜骑士·出击』；\n3、自身拥有茄子骑士时，触发处于『茄之紫』状态的『蔬菜骑士·出击』；\n4、自身未拥有蔬菜骑士时，不触发『蔬菜骑士·出击』。=Based on the following priority, YUI will activate a different [Vegetable Knight: Strike] after using HIGHLIGHT:\n1. When the HIGHLIGHT target isn't inflicted with [Mushroom Spores] and YUI has Mushroom Knight, activate [Mushroom Pink] state [Vegetable Knight: Strike];\n2. When YUI doesn't have [Tuber Power] and has Potato Knight, activate [Potato Yellow] state [Vegetable Knight: Strike];\n3. When YUI has Eggplant Knight, activate [Eggplant Purple] state [Vegetable Knight: Strike];\n4. When YUI has no Vegetable Knights, do not activate [Vegetable Knight: Strike].
按下述优先顺序，{{A}}在释放HIGHLIGHT后会触发处于不同状态下的『蔬菜战士·出击』：\n1、HIGHLIGHT目标未处于『蘑菇孢子』状态下，且自身拥有蘑菇骑士时，触发处于『菇之粉』状态的『蔬菜战士·出击』；\n2、自身未处于『块茎之力』状态下，且自身拥有马铃薯骑士时，触发处于『薯之黄』状态的『蔬菜战士·出击』；\n3、自身拥有茄子骑士时，触发处于『茄之紫』状态的『蔬菜战士·出击』；\n4、自身未拥有蔬菜骑士时，不触发『蔬菜战士·出击』。=Based on the following priority, YUI will activate a different [Vegetable Knight: Strike] after using HIGHLIGHT:\n1. When the HIGHLIGHT target isn't inflicted with [Mushroom Spores] and YUI has Mushroom Knight, activate [Mushroom Pink] state [Vegetable Knight: Strike];\n2. When YUI doesn't have [Tuber Power] and has Potato Knight, activate [Potato Yellow] state [Vegetable Knight: Strike];\n3. When YUI has Eggplant Knight, activate [Eggplant Purple] state [Vegetable Knight: Strike];\n4. When YUI has no Vegetable Knights, do not activate [Vegetable Knight: Strike].

<color\=#66ccff>『愿望聆听』</color>=<color\=#66ccff>[Wish Listener]</color>

<color\=#66ccff>『神谕转换』</color>=<color\=#66ccff>[Oracle Shift]</color>
r:"^消耗(\d+)层『愿望聆听』，使当前回合所属的友方角色（后称『当前角色』）暂时退场并使『后备角色』登场并进行1次行动，『后备角色』行动后退场并重新替换为『当前角色』，『当前角色』继续行动。\n『后备角色』登场时，会复制『当前角色』非自身添加的所有状态（『后备角色』退场时会清除这些状态）。『后备角色』初次登场时，会触发所有"战斗开始时"的效果。『后备角色』退场时，所有状态的持续时间不会减少。$"="Spend $1 [Wish Listener] stacks. The acting [Current Character] become inactive, the [Backup Character] become active and take 1 action. After this action, the [Backup Character] become inactive, and the [Current Character] become active to continue their turn. \nWhen the [Backup Character] is active, they copy all status effects from the [Current Character] except those they applied to themselves. These are cleared when the [Backup Character] become inactive. When the [Backup Character] first become active, activate all [Start of Battle] effects. When the [Backup Character] become inactive, do not affect the duration of effects with turn limits."
<color\=#66ccff>战斗轮次</color>=<color\=#66ccff>Combat Turn</color>
战斗中所有存活的友方角色都经过了1次非额外回合后，视为经过了1次战斗轮次。=After all alive allies take 1 non-Extra Action action, count as 1 combat turn.
战斗中所有存活的友方角色都经过了1次回合后，视为经过了1次战斗轮次。=After all alive allies take 1 action, count as 1 combat turn.
<color\=#66ccff>后备角色</color>=<color\=#66ccff>Backup Character</color>
只在队伍上阵{{A}}后，可以选择一名未上阵的可使用角色作为{{A}}的『后备角色』；『后备角色』不视作编入队伍，不计入战斗开局的属性、职业、角色数量等；=Only after {{A}} is in the party, you can select 1 non-deployed character as {{A}}'s [Backup Character]; The [Backup Character] don't count as being in the party, and will not interact with start of battle attribute, role, character number, etc;
仅在队伍上阵{{A}}后，可以选择一名未上阵的可使用角色作为{{A}}的『后备角色』；『后备角色』不视作编入队伍，不计入战斗开局的属性、职业、角色数量等；=Only after {{A}} is in the party, you can select 1 non-deployed character as {{A}}'s [Backup Character]; The [Backup Character] don't count as being in the party, and will not interact with start of battle attribute, role, character number, etc;

<color\=#66ccff>面具强度</color>=<color\=#66ccff>Desire Level</color>
{{A}}&{{B}}的特色属性，会影响释放{{A}}&{{B}}技能部分效果的强度。=Influences the effects of certain skills based on stacks.
<color\=#66ccff>技能效果增幅</color>=<color\=#66ccff>Skill Effect Amp</color>
使{{A}}技能/战斗技巧中技能升级项的技能强度提升，该效果与其他加成效果独立计算。对“受到角色属性影响的效果”生效时，不会提升属性的计入上限而直接对技能强度生效。=Increase the effects of skills/Thief Tactics that are increased when levelling up skills. This effect is calculated independently of other effects. For effects that influences the Phantom Thieves' stats, the stats increase cap will not be raised, but instead be applied directly as a skill effect.
<color\=#66ccff>相貌</color>=<color\=#66ccff>Facade</color>
{{A}}&{{B}}的特色资源，不同的相貌组合可以触发技能『二元合一的面具』不同的效果。=The effects of [Two Masks as One] change depending on the combination of Facades gained.
<color\=#66ccff>进阶属性</color>=<color\=#66ccff>Effects Stats</color>
包含暴击率、暴击效果、穿透、伤害加成、弱点伤害等，可在角色属性介面查看全部属性。=Effect stats include Crit Rate, Crit DMG, Pierce, DMG Bonus, Weak DMG, and more.

<color\=#66ccff>『光影流转』</color>=<color\=#66ccff>[Flowing Light]</color>
{{A}}的特殊战斗资源。释放『黄昏之余晖』消耗『光影流转』时会同时触发消耗『光』与『影』的效果。={{A}}'s special resource. When spending [Flowing Light] from [Twilight Radiance], the effects of [Light] and [Shadow] will both activate.
<color\=#66ccff>固定伤害</color>=<color\=#66ccff>Fixed Damage</color>
固定数值的伤害，不受任何作用于伤害的加成效果影响（如伤害加成、攻击力加成、暴击率等）。=The damage is a fixed value and is not affected by any damage-boosting effects (such as DMG Bonus, ATK Bonus, Crit Rate, etc).
<color\=#66ccff>『决意的少女』</color>=<color\=#66ccff>[Resolute Maiden]</color>
{{A}}的特殊状态。进入『决意的少女』状态后，释放HIGHLIGHT时技能倍率提升。={{A}}'s special state. After entering [Resolute Maiden], when activating a HIGHLIGHT, increase skill multiplier.
<color\=#66ccff>『闪络』</color>=<color\=#66ccff>[Flashover]</color>
{{A}}主动释放『瞬雷枪击』时为敌人添加的负面状态，使敌人受到伤害提升。={{A}} can inflict this debuff when directly using [Thunder Thrust], increase foes' DMG Taken.
